texlive-roboto in fedora-32

This page displays detail informations of the texlive-roboto package. You might want go back to the main page of texlive-roboto.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2021-03-08 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-35 - update texlive-subfiles and fix dependencies
2020-12-07 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-34 - put the /usr/share/fonts/tex-gyre symlink back in
2020-11-23 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-33 - do not make fonts symlink for texlive-merriweather (conflicts with sorkintype-merriweather-fonts)
2020-11-10 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-32 - fix platex file ownership
2020-11-02 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-31 - update the following fonts: * algolrevived * almendra * baskervillef * bitter * cabin * cochineal * domitian * erewhon * etbb * fbb * forum * garamond-libre * libertinus * libertinus-fonts * libertinus-otf * libertinus-type1 * libertinust1math * librebaskerville * librecaslon * lobster2 * marcellus * merriweather * newtx * newtxsf * overlock * playfair * quattrocento * scholax * xcharter - add these new fonts: * cmathbb * courierten * ibarra * josefin * notomath * plimsoll * spectral - and update the default font map files to match (texlive-updmap-map)
2020-10-23 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-30 - move all the big Obsoletes over to fedora-obsolete-packages (f34+ only)
2020-10-23 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-29 - drop Requires: texlive-obsoletes (so fedora-obsolete-packages can handle it)
2020-10-19 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-28 - Recommends: tex(splitidx.sty) for texlive-imakeidx
2020-07-29 Fedora Release Engineering - 9:2020-27 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_33_Mass_Rebuild
2020-07-09 Tom Callaway - 9:2020-26 - update svg to latest (to fix issues with inkscape -z) - fix dependencies on tuda-ci - fix provides on urcls
